        * @param testName : string name of test is ADTK experiment config (not necessarily same as abacus name)
        * @param validToLog : boolean to verify test to be logged as CMPTST var. Usually a check that parent test is 1
        * @param childValue : int bucket value of abacus test
        * @param checkControl : boolean that DFP call should request a MARQUEECONTROL adunit.
        *    this adunit is only to be used if correctly targetted in DFP to this CMPTST.
        * @param controlValues : array of integer bucket IDs for which to use MARQUEECONTROL adunit
        *    if no values are specified, and checkControl is true, all buckets will use MARQUEECONTROL if they request a MARQUEE adunit
        *
        * @access useControlMarquee boolean true if MARQUEE adunit should be re-written as MARQUEECONTROL
        * @access child : int ID of childTest
        * @access name : string name of test in ADTK experiment config
        * @access value : int bucket of childTest
        * @access validToLog : boolean if test is to be logged as CMPTST
        * @access cmptst : string CMPTST value (childID.bucket eg 12345.1)
        */
       function ABTest(childId, testName, validToLog, childValue, checkControl, controlValues) {
         this.child = childId;
         this.name = testName;
         this.value = isNaN(childValue) ? -1 : childValue;
         this.validToLog = validToLog || false;
         this.useControlMarquee = (checkControl === true) && (controlValues.length === 0 || controlValues.indexOf(this.value) >= 0);
         this.cmptst = this.child + '.' + this.value;
       }
       var tests = [];
 
       /* add parent child tests below: */
       tests.push(new ABTest(25669, "TVLY_PintWizard_Child", false, 0, true, [0]));
       tests.push(new ABTest(26075, "TVLY_NativeMarquee_Child", false, 0, true, [0]));
 
       marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting = marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting || {};
       var CMPTSTs = [];
       var useControl = false;
       if (marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting.CMPTST) {
         CMPTSTs.push(marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting.CMPTST);
       }
       for (var t in tests) {
         if (tests[t].validToLog === true) {
           if (CMPTSTs.indexOf(tests[t].cmptst) < 0) {
             CMPTSTs.push(tests[t].cmptst);
             if (tests[t].useControlMarquee && marqueeAdConfig.adCalls && marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[marqueeAdConfig.adToLoad]) {
               useControl = true;
             }
           }
         }
       }
       if(useControl) {
         var OLDPATH = 'MARQUEE';
         var NEWPATH = 'MARQUEECONTROL';
         var adPage = marqueeAdConfig.adToLoad;
         var url = marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].url;
         var path = marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].path;
         if (url) {
           marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].url = url.replace(OLDPATH, NEWPATH);
         }
         if (path) {
           marqueeAdConfig.adCalls[adPage].path = path.replace(OLDPATH, NEWPATH);
         }
       }
       if(CMPTSTs.length > 0) {
         marqueeAdConfig.updatedTargeting.CMPTST = CMPTSTs.join(',');
       }
 
       function postMarqueeLoadedCallBack(slot) {
           if (slot && slot.selector && (slot.selector === '#hero-banner' || slot.selector === '#WizardHero :first-child')) {
           if (!slot.devices) {
             expads.utils.toggleCollapsedExpanded(document.querySelector(slot.selector), false);
           }
           var log = false;
           if (log && window.dctk && typeof(window.dctk.evaluateExperimentAndLog) === 'function') {
             var params = {};
             params.id = 26075;
             if (window.dctk.omtr && window.dctk.omtr.pageName) {
               params.pageName = window.dctk.omtr.pageName;
             } else if (window.dctk._pageName) {
               params.pageName = window.dctk._pageName;
             }
             params.eapid = window.dctk._eapid;
             params.tpid = window.dctk._tpid;
             params.guid = window.dctk._guid;
             window.dctk.evaluateExperimentAndLog(params)
           }
         }
       }
 
       if (expads.events && expads.events.postMarqueeImageLoaded) {
         expads.events.postMarqueeImageLoaded.attachHandler(postMarqueeLoadedCallBack);
       } else if (expads.events && expads.events.postMarqueeCallSuccess) {
         expads.events.postMarqueeCallSuccess.attachHandler(postMarqueeLoadedCallBack);
       }
 
       return marqueeAdConfig;
     });
   </script>

      <section class="flex-module editorial default-view" data-fm="606991" id="editorial-1">
       <div class="box editorial">
        <div class="uitk-grid all-x-gutter-12 flex-tile flex-same-height cols-nested wrapper-toggle " data-flex-flip="">
         <div class="uitk-col editorial-result-card " data-fm-content="11581370">
          <div class="flex-card">
           <div class="flex-content">
            <div class="flex-area-primary">
             <div class="flex-app-content">
              <h1 style="color: rgb(31, 31, 31);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Australia's First Online Booking Site For Travel
              </h1>
              <h4 style="color: rgb(31, 31, 31);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               What (or wot) is Wotif?
              </h4>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               The universe is full of questions. What is the meaning of life? Where do socks go when they disappear from the dryer? But the most important question right now is: What in the world is Wotif?
              </p>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Well, we’re not a bird, we’re not a plane, and we’re fairly certain we’re not Superman. Instead, we’re an online travel company dedicated to getting you from here to there without throwing your wallet to the wolves. And we’re pretty good at it, too! That’s why 1 in 2 Aussies have travelled with us since 2000. That’s a lot of happy campers! And jetsetters... and honeymooners... and road trippers... and gap year-ers...
              </p>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               The Wotif story is different to those of other hotel booking sites. We were founded in a Brisbane garage (seriously) and have heaps of local knowledge. We use it to track down fantastic travel deals so you can find awesome deals every day. And we’re not just talking about accommodation. With Wotif, you can book everything in one place: flights, hotels, packages, and activities. Talk about a time saver!
              </p>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Oh, and did we mention our
               <span>
               </span>
               <a href="https://www.wotif.com/p/home-of-holidays" style="background-color: transparent;color: rgb(30, 111, 168);">
                Price Promise
               </a>
               ? It covers ALL our hotels and packages, so if you find a cheaper price within 24 hours of booking with us, we’ll match it by refunding the difference*. How good is that?
              </p>
              <h4 style="color: rgb(31, 31, 31);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Hotels, Flights, and Packages - Oh My!
              </h4>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Looking for
               <span>
               </span>
               <a href="https://www.wotif.com/Sydney-Hotels.d178312.Travel-Guide-Hotels" style="background-color: transparent;color: rgb(30, 111, 168);">
                Sydney accommodation
               </a>
               ,
               <span>
               </span>
               <a href="https://www.wotif.com/Melbourne-Hotels.d178283.Travel-Guide-Hotels" style="background-color: transparent;color: rgb(30, 111, 168);">
                Melbourne accommodation
               </a>
               <span>
               </span>
               or
               <span>
               </span>
               <a href="https://www.wotif.com/Gold-Coast-Hotels.d180064.Travel-Guide-Hotels" style="background-color: transparent;color: rgb(30, 111, 168);">
                Gold Coast hotels
               </a>
               ? Wotif’s got you covered. Need a
               <span>
               </span>
               <a href="https://www.wotif.com/Bali-Hotels.d602651.Travel-Guide-Hotels" style="background-color: transparent;color: rgb(30, 111, 168);">
                hotel in Bali
               </a>
               <span>
               </span>
               or some spectacular
               <span>
               </span>
               <a href="https://www.wotif.com/Phuket-Hotels.d6046393.Travel-Guide-Hotels" style="background-color: transparent;color: rgb(30, 111, 168);">
                Phuket accommodation
               </a>
               ? Look no further. London stays, New York getaways, NZ adventures – you’ve come to the right place. 5-star luxury resorts, romantic bed-and-breakfasts, funky backpacker hostels... you name it, Wotif’s got it.
              </p>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               But Wotif offers more than just top hotel deals (although we do have stacks of ‘em). Our mantra is “Everything travel. Everyday deals. Local knowledge.” That means epic flight deals, awesome activities, essential travel insurance, handy car rentals, and super easy, cash-saving packages every day. It means more than 1.5 million hotel reviews from Aussie travellers like you (trust us, you don’t want to count them). And it means you’ll save even more when you book your whole trip with us. Yep – bundle your accommodation and flight together as a Wotif package and we’ll give you an extra discount on your hotel. Or book your flight first to unlock 10 days of special hotel deals. Either way, your hotel or package is still covered by our Price Promise.
              </p>
              <h4 style="color: rgb(31, 31, 31);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Don't Waste Time Searching
              </h4>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               Searching the internet for deals on travel and spending hours comparing travel sites is about as exciting as watching paint dry. Grey paint. On a really boring wall. So why not save your time and cash by booking everything you need on Wotif? Our online hotel booking service is awesome, and our Price Promise means you don’t have to shop around. So what are you waiting for? For a holiday packed with value, book now with Wotif.com!
              </p>
              <p style="color: rgb(64, 64, 64);background-color: rgb(255, 255, 255);">
               *Eligibility requirements and conditions apply.
              </p>
             </div>

             var mobileSuppress = function() {
                 var isiPad = navigator.userAgent.match(/iPad/i) != null;
                 var isMobile = navigator.userAgent.match(/Mobile|Android|BlackBerry/i) != null;
                 return (isMobile && !isiPad);
             };
 
             var overrideForBacktab = function () {
                 //overriding the condition for mobile devices only.
                 if (exitWindowConfig.backTabEnabledForMobile && mobileSuppress()) {
                     $.each(exitWindowConfig, function (key, value) {
                         if (key === "hotel" || key === "shortTermHotelOnly") {
                             exitWindowConfig[key] = "intentmedia";
                         }
                     });
                 }
             };
 
             overrideForBacktab();
             if (mobileSuppress()) {
                 exitWindowConfig.deviceEnabled = false;
             }
             if ((conditionizr.ie8 || conditionizr.ie9|| conditionizr.ie10|| conditionizr.ie11 ||
                     conditionizr.safari || conditionizr.firefox)) {
                 exitWindowConfig.browserEnabled = true;
             }
 
             var removeObjectProperties = function(obj, props) {
                 for (var i = 0; i < props.length; i++) {
                     if (obj.hasOwnProperty(props[i])) {
                         delete obj[props[i]];
                     }
                 }
             };
 
             if (exitWindowConfig.siteEnabled) {
                 exitWindowConfig.enabled = (exitWindowConfig.deviceEnabled && exitWindowConfig.browserEnabled);
                 if (conditionizr.ie8 || conditionizr.ie9|| conditionizr.ie10|| conditionizr.ie11) {

                         if (value === "popunder") {
                             exitWindowConfig[key] = "";

                             exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                         } else if (key === "shortTermHotelOnly" && value === "hotwire" && window.locale !== "en_US") {
                             exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                         }
                     });
                 }
 
                 conditionizr.on('safari', function () {
                     $.each(exitWindowConfig, function(key, value){
                         if (value === "popunder") {
                             exitWindowConfig[key] = value + "UnfocusedTab";
                         } else if ((key === "hotel" || key === "shortTermHotelOnly") && value === "hotwire") {
                             exitWindowConfig[key] = value + "UnfocusedTab";
                         }
                     });
                 });

                     $.each(exitWindowConfig, function(key, value){
                         if (key === "hotel" && (value !== "hotwire" && value !== "intentmedia")) {
                             exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                         }
                     });
                 });
 
                 conditionizr.on('chrome', function () {

                                 exitWindowConfig[key] = "";
                             }
                         }
                     });
                 });
 
                 removeObjectProperties(exitWindowConfig, ["deviceEnabled", "browserEnabled"]);
